‡∏Ç‡∏≠ Quote ‡∏•‡∏∏‡∏á George Carlin ‡πÉ‡∏ô‡∏ï‡∏≥‡∏ô‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏°‡∏≤‡∏ô‡∏∞‡∏Ñ‡∏∞

" (some jokes) Don't seem right, but you can joke about it. I believe you can joke about anything. It all depends on how you construct the joke and what the exaggeration is. Because every joke needs one exaggeration; every joke needs one thing to be way out of proportion."
